  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_7a8a01ea-9d13-4e53-8b88-03eb3d98a67e'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText10662074007789997730" style="display:none"><i>Alternate cover edition, ISBN:<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18068464" rel="nofollow noopener">9780989527415</a></i><br /><br />Fifty years ago The Commander came into power and murdered all who opposed him. In his warped mind, the seven deadly sins were the downfall of society. <br /><br />To punish the guilty, he created the Hole, a place where sinners are branded according to their sins. Sinners are forced to live a less than human existence in deplorable conditions, under the watchful eye of guards who are ready to kill anyone who steps out of line.<br /><br />Now, LUST wraps around my neck like thick, blue fingers, threatening to choke the life out of me. I’ve been accused of a crime I didn’t commit, and the Hole is my new home. <br /><br />Constant darkness. <br /><br />Brutal and savage violence. <br /><br />Excruciating pain. <br /><br />Every day is a fight for survival. <br /><br />But I won’t let them win.     <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer544185681" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9388591902370970633"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410875i/806259._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410875i/806260._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410875i/806261.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote> <i> <b> "I love you... I don't want you to ever question it. I'd give up my life for yours. That's how much I love you. Don't you dare ever doubt that." </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br/>WOW!!!<br/><br/><b> Fast paced, action-packed and emotionally charged, Branded is a phenomenal Dystopian debut with a forbidden romance that will capture your heart! A must-read of 2013! </b><br/><br/>The writing was strong, I fell in love with the characters and was totally wrapped up in the world. There was a swoon-worthy hero, a strong heroine, a forbidden romance (and I</span>
  <span id="freeText9388591902370970633" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410875i/806259._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410875i/806260._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410875i/806261.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote> <i> <b> "I love you... I don't want you to ever question it. I'd give up my life for yours. That's how much I love you. Don't you dare ever doubt that." </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br>WOW!!!<br><br><b> Fast paced, action-packed and emotionally charged, Branded is a phenomenal Dystopian debut with a forbidden romance that will capture your heart! A must-read of 2013! </b><br><br>The writing was strong, I fell in love with the characters and was totally wrapped up in the world. There was a swoon-worthy hero, a strong heroine, a forbidden romance (and I mean REALLY forbidden) and a super evil bad guy. Now, I don't normally read Dystopians but this one had me HOOKED!!!<br><br>In a society where Sinners of the seven deadly sins are branded and incarcerated, everyone's lives are always at risk. It didn't matter than Lexi was innocent and it made no difference what she said. She was accused, condemned and thrown into The Hole - a hellish, filthy, self-contained prison with no rules and no way out.<br><br><blockquote> <i> "I don't want to die, but at the same time, I wish I were dead." </i>
</blockquote> <br>She was assigned a guard - Cole. But there was more to him than met the eye. Something about him was different than all the other guards. Something in him was good. And, as she slowly acclimatizes to her new life in the Hole, they grew closer and closer.<br><br>But in the Hole, relations between Guards and Sinners is punishable by torture and death. It is final, it is brutal and it is the world they live in. But... they're still falling for each other. Hard.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> "I never planned on falling for you. You were just an assignment. But it just sort of happened and now... There's not a single thing I would change about you. When you smile, my entire world stops. All I see is you. I need you." </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410875i/806262._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't even know where to start with how much I loved this! It was a total change of pace for me because I never usually read Dystopian books. I mean, I read the Hunger Games, but that was it. I guess I just generally prefer books that focus more strongly on romance. But sometimes you want more than just a romance, you know? You want a bit of an adventure... something thrilling and different that'll sweep you away into another world and Branded delivered that.<br><br>It was a non-stop roller coaster ride. My emotions were all over the place. Fear. Disgust. Betrayal. Love. Swoon (yes, swoon is an emotion). Despair. Hope. It had my heart in knots and I loved every minute of it!<br><br>Now I know the story is classified as mature YA but let me tell you, it is gory, gruesome and gritty!! Certainly not for the faint of heart! I swear, there is this one flashback scene that I'm going to need therapy after reading!! But, that being said, that grittiness was so effective in pulling you right into the world. The world itself was gritty and you felt it.<br><br>I swooned pretty hard over Cole. In fact, let me take a minute here to shout this: I LOVE COLE!!!! The forbidden angle gave the romance such a thrill to it. You could see him fighting his feelings for her. Being so badass and protective of her. But there was so much more at stake than just their feelings. There were just so many layers dictating all of their actions as they lived under the constant fear of punishment by death simply for the crime of falling in love. Mess up and die. Fall in love and die.<br><br><blockquote> <i> "He takes my face into his hand, and reassures me. "So outside of these walls, we can't stand each other." </i>
</blockquote>  <br>But you see their bond grow and it's scary because you're both rooting for their relationship and just terrified because you see first hand the consequences of a relationship between a Guard and Sinner. There was so much swoon and so much fear!<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> "The last thing I want is for you to be afraid of me. But I want you to trust me. I need you to trust me." He sighs and I hear the pain and confusion in his voice.<br><br>"Why?"<br><br>"I don't know why and it scares the hell out of me." He swallows hard...<br><br>Part of me screams for him to run for his own safety, but I don't want him to move. My heart begs... Please stay with me. Forever." </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br>Lexi was a strong, wonderful heroine you couldn't help but sympathize with. She was a fighter at her heart but everything in her life just kept kicking her down. I loved seeing her strength grow over the course of the book. <br><br><blockquote> <i> "You won't break me if that's what you're worries about."<br>He walks over, places one arm around my back, and lifts me...<br>"After this, I'm not sure anyone could," he whispers." </i>
</blockquote>  <br>Now, relationship-wise this book is YA in that there is no sex in it. But this is one of those stories where the connection between the hero/heroine is so strong that the descriptions of their actions doesn't need to be graphic for you to FEEL it. Like there's this scene, after a fight and he's just washing blood off her hand (not even something romantic per say) but ohhhhh myyyy God did it make my heart clench! Seriously. I FELT it. <br><br><blockquote> <i> "Shhh..." He grips me closer to his body and then softly whispers in my ear, "I'm about to kiss you, and once I start I won't be able to stop. Just thought I should warn you." </i>
</blockquote> <br>And this whole relationship is developing in the midst of a world with daily gun fights in the streets, explosions, rapes, murders, injustice and a world under the dictatorship of an evil Commander.<br><br>The book is not all dark and grit though. There were definitely happy moments that shone through the darkness showing that even in this pit of absolute despair, there were still people with good in their hearts! But holy hell!! There were also a few scenes that just rendered me speechless with how nightmarish they were! I loved that there was a bit of everything in this book though. The plot was full of twists and turns and was fast paced enough that you were always reading about something new and yet took it's time enough that you were able to develop a close connection to the characters.<br><br>And I just want to point out that Branded has THE awesomest dog EVER in it. His name is Zeus, he belongs to Cole (though he's pretty sure he belongs to Lexi) and I seriously adore him and could not review this book without sending him a shout out.<br><br>Don't forget though that this IS a dystopian. There's fighting, battles, rebellions, and a whole story outside of the romance but for those of you who are hard-core romance fans, Cole and Lexi's relationship will keep you turning the pages to find out what happens to them.<br><br>The ending is thankfully NOT a cliffhanger!! They were together and safe, for now at least. Their story is far from over but my heart can rest easy for now while I eagerly await book #2.<br><br>Fans of the Hunger Games absolutely MUST read this but know that, in my opinion, Branded knocks The Hunger Games out of the water!<br><br>Abi Ketner and Missy Kalicicki are an author power team to watch out for!<br><br>I can't wait for more from the Sinners series and to find out what happens next with Lexi and Cole!<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> "Just leave me," I whisper in his ear.<br>"Never." </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br><br><u> Expected release: June 28, 2013.</u><br><br><b> Want to read the first chapter? Trust me, you'll be hooked too: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://aestasbookblog.com/branded-sinners-series">http://aestasbookblog.com/branded-sin...</a><br><br><b> CASTING (see above and below):<br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410875i/806263._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410875i/806264._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410875i/806265._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> Darkness. Death. Violence. Pain. <br><br>Now, everyday is a fight for survival. But I won’t die. I won’t let them win.<br><br>The Hole can’t keep me. The Hole can’t break me. <br><br>I am more than my brand. I’m a fighter. <br><br>My name is Lexi Hamilton, and this is my story. </i><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410875i/806266._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></b></b></b></span>

<div id="review_637202498" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/637202498" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/637202498?book_show_action=true">Jun 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=z-no-bueno">z-no-bueno</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=everyone-loved-but-duchess">everyone-loved-but-duchess</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=heroine-tstl">heroine-tstl</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=new-authors-review">new-authors-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-ya-dystopian">genre-ya-dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=arc-for-review">arc-for-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-new-adult">genre-new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=arc-net-galley">arc-net-galley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer637202498" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13553996500707736438">2.5 Stars. Sad Face :(<br/><br/>This book has SO MUCH PROMISE. The premise is awesome, and no matter how many YA dystopian I read, I love them all. So I was really excited to get this from Net Galley, especially after all of the raving reviews. But I feel like once I missed something that everyone else seemed to get. WHAT AM I NOT GETTING? This book started off strong and exciting but the appeal quickly turned to confusion and boredom for me.<br/><br/>One big problem was the characterization of both Lexi and Cole. </span>
  <span id="freeText13553996500707736438" style="display:none">2.5 Stars. Sad Face :(<br /><br />This book has SO MUCH PROMISE. The premise is awesome, and no matter how many YA dystopian I read, I love them all. So I was really excited to get this from Net Galley, especially after all of the raving reviews. But I feel like once I missed something that everyone else seemed to get. WHAT AM I NOT GETTING? This book started off strong and exciting but the appeal quickly turned to confusion and boredom for me.<br /><br />One big problem was the characterization of both Lexi and Cole. Lexi enters page one trying to hang herself...literally has a rope wrapped around her neck, ready to jump. That's when the bad guys come to drag her off to the Hole to be branded with the brand of the sin of lust. Instead of completing her goal, she gets the urge to live and runs away...to no avail, of course. This is explained later as a will to be able to CHOOSE how she goes out, not to be forced into it. Okay, I can somewhat understand that. Now on her way to the Hole, she hardens herself and wants to maintain her dignity...these evil people will NOT get her down! And yet she proceeds to whine and simper and swoon and shake and cower and cringe at nearly everything that happens to her. Cole steps in as her guard/love interest, and good grief does he ever have his work cut out for him! Even so, Lexi proceeds to become a competent worker, then back to a helpless damsel in distress, running up the stairs alone when she should be staying put, openly defying her protectors and doing things she is forbidden to do, etc...She started becoming the idiot girl in a B movie, going into the dark stairway with nothing but a flashlight and her boobs to protect her. But...wait for it...by the end of the book, Lexi is a badass fighter girl who has only trained for a week but somehow becomes some kind of tactical expert. It was just wierd. I know I went on a bit here, but I'm just trying to get my point across. Who IS Lexi? Is she the lonely, desperate girl, the competent nurse, the stupid, helpless bimbo, or the badass fighter?<br /><br />Cole also remained much a mystery throughout the story. Not only did not understand what he saw in Lexi, but I couldn't understand what she saw in him, either. There is no background info on him, no explanation of why he has chosen to hold to his morals. He's just there, and he's hot, and he doesn't try to rape Lexi. GIRL IS IN LOOOOOVE!!!!! After being with Cole for a couple of weeks, Lexi falls so desperately in love with him that she is destitute when he has to be gone for a few days...literally <b>cannot function</b> without him. And this is while she is a nurse in a hospital. I'm in nursing school myself...I say, bye bye Lexi, you weak willed little girl! No need to ignore your patients because your boyfriend is gone away working for a bit. Go back to junior high and try healing people when you've grown up a bit.<br /><br />The last thing I'll mention is the timing of...well, basically everything. I'm still confused as to the actual time frame that everything happened in, but as far as I could tell, it all happened within a couple of months. Let me tell you, Lexi gets her ass handed to her a handful of times...they literally beat her unconscious more than once, and she sustains multiple head injuries during her short stay in the Hole. At one point, she has something like <b>26 STAPLES IN HER HEAD,</b> which are taken out two days later. HUH?!?!?!?! Did I read that wrong? The doctor is telling her how he was picking bone fragments of her skull out of her head while he was stapling her, and mentions that she <i>might</i> have a concussion. Hahaha! I'd say that's a big ten four, good buddy...and I'd also advise you to keep those staples in her head for a wee bit longer, otherwise what's the point?<br /><br />I'm done now. I know that once again, I'm in the vast minority with my opinion. I simply don't understand all the five star reviews, because I find the flaws in this book very obvious. I think the second book might still be on my radar, which I would never normally do when I had this many issues with a book. But I honestly feel as if the writing was just very juvenile and unpolished. I think the author had a fabulous idea and an amazing world to put her characters through. She doesn't hesitate to be brutal, and she's not overly loyal to her characters. That's definitely a positive point for me, because the book was somewhat unpredictable. But in the end, I didn't care much for either Lexi or Cole, because they never became real to me. Their characters were too wishy washy, and the melodrama was over the top by <u>miles and miles.</u> If there had been more introspection, maybe some insight into what makes each of them tick, what it is that draws them together, I'd feel more for them.<br /><br />Arc provided by the publisher via Net Galley.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13553996500707736438" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/614278799?book_show_action=true">May 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer614278799" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12082405920309928401"><b>5+++ AMAZING STARS!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/f2a2acbb-4ac4-4ca9-a591-aa926c4b7cf8_zpsac2bb85f.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421413i/837063._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo f2a2acbb-4ac4-4ca9-a591-aa926c4b7cf8_zpsac2bb85f.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>What can I say about this book... I feel like anything I write isn’t going to do it justice. I read it 4 or 5 days ago and I’m STILL trying to come up with something good enough. I was blown away. Incredible, Phenomenal, Amazing... those are the first words that pop into my head! This is one of those books I will be recommending to anyone and everyone! <br/><br/>This is Lexi’s story. <br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/76dd988c-7711-47cc-97d7-ab5f6ffc63cf_zps691ceca4.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421413i/837064.jpg' alt=' photo 76dd988c-7711-47cc-97d7-ab5f6ffc63cf_zps691ceca4.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>The world is different now. Years ago, after WWV, the justice system was revamped by ‘The Comm</span>
  <span id="freeText12082405920309928401" style="display:none"><b>5+++ AMAZING STARS!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/f2a2acbb-4ac4-4ca9-a591-aa926c4b7cf8_zpsac2bb85f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421413i/837063._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo f2a2acbb-4ac4-4ca9-a591-aa926c4b7cf8_zpsac2bb85f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>What can I say about this book... I feel like anything I write isn’t going to do it justice. I read it 4 or 5 days ago and I’m STILL trying to come up with something good enough. I was blown away. Incredible, Phenomenal, Amazing... those are the first words that pop into my head! This is one of those books I will be recommending to anyone and everyone! <br><br>This is Lexi’s story. <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/76dd988c-7711-47cc-97d7-ab5f6ffc63cf_zps691ceca4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421413i/837064.jpg" alt=" photo 76dd988c-7711-47cc-97d7-ab5f6ffc63cf_zps691ceca4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The world is different now. Years ago, after WWV, the justice system was revamped by ‘The Commander.’ People no longer have trials, there is no ‘innocent until proven guilty.’ If you are accused, you are automatically a Sinner and placed in the Hole. It doesn’t matter if it’s true or not, thats just the way it is. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/41a3fdf9-b9a8-4437-ac86-28b8bd952f9d_zps01613db7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421413i/837065._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 41a3fdf9-b9a8-4437-ac86-28b8bd952f9d_zps01613db7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Once at the Hole, you get Branded. It is a painful process. You will forever be identified by your sin. <br><b>At what point do they believe what’s been branded on their skin instead of just knowing who they are inside?</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/ca71127c-5fd6-42f0-baa3-65077aa8c04f_zps863318a0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421413i/837066.jpg" alt=" photo ca71127c-5fd6-42f0-baa3-65077aa8c04f_zps863318a0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The Commander is under the impression that these seven sins lead to the destruction of civilization, so if you are accused of one, you are branded that color. Lexi is branded blue. She is wrongfully accused, but she doesn’t stand up for herself. Would it matter if she did? Probably not. She has her reasons for not fighting...<br><i>The Hole had to be better than the hell she was already living in.</i>  <br><br>Each of the Sinners are assigned a guard. It is the guards responsibility to make sure the Sinner stays in line, gets to work and back etc. Having a guard doesn’t mean much in the Hole. People die every day. <br>Lexi’s guards name is Cole. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/64a52598-c012-4117-b2a3-ecebf12c8d45_zps773f90bd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421413i/837067.jpg" alt=" photo 64a52598-c012-4117-b2a3-ecebf12c8d45_zps773f90bd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Cole is <b>amazing</b>. If Lexi had any other guard besides Cole, she would be doomed. Cole figures out pretty quickly that Lexi is different than most of the other Sinners. Cole is most definitely different than other guards. He shows that pretty quickly with how he treats Lexi, and the things he does for her (Alyssa ♥). They start to fall for one another. But it’s not safe for either one. Relationships between Sinners and guards have severe punishment. Torture. Death. The feelings they have for one another are scary. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/bee14376-233e-405e-93cc-df373d2eb603_zps4960bcb0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421413i/837068.jpg" alt=" photo bee14376-233e-405e-93cc-df373d2eb603_zps4960bcb0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The consequences of them being together could be dire. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I never planned on falling for you. You were just an assignment. But it just sort of happened and now look where I am. Stuck between two walls that won’t budge either way. I’m trapped by you and my obligations as a guard.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>It’s official. Cole stole my heart. There is just something about this guy, he had me swooning like no other. He was protective of Lexi from the beginning. The things that came out of his mouth...<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/045e8d35-71b2-442f-b23b-625b73fb964e_zps5aceebd4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421413i/837069.jpg" alt=" photo 045e8d35-71b2-442f-b23b-625b73fb964e_zps5aceebd4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You showed me what it’s like to really care about a person for the first time in my life, and now that I have you, I’m not going to let you go.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Lexi is one of the toughest heroines I have ever come across. She has been through so much in her life, yet she still is able to survive, to love, to help. She is a courageous. She is a survivor. <br><b>
  <blockquote>Whatever the cost, I’ll fight. This is as ready as I’ll ever be.</blockquote>
</b><br>The relationship between Cole and Lexi was a big part of the book, but there was another part just as big. There is a war going on. The people of the Hole are fighting back. There is destruction, violence, etc. This is not a happy story. It can be down right gruesome at times, but its also very beautiful. Lexi has a choice to make. For her- the choice is easy. If Lexi has any chance of getting free, of being with Cole, she has to fight. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/e34e70c3-a496-433d-b991-161b5fe73573_zpsbab9322c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421413i/837070.jpg" alt=" photo e34e70c3-a496-433d-b991-161b5fe73573_zpsbab9322c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There were so many twists and turns at the end, some things I really didn’t see coming. I had so much going on the day I read this, but every thing else went on hold. I couldn’t stop reading once I picked this up, and you won’t be able to either. The ending wasn’t a cliffhanger, but I am still very anxious to read the second installment! <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/8ed11472-0272-4ae8-aee7-5e0ad394b426_zpsc8ba4baa.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421413i/837071.jpg" alt=" photo 8ed11472-0272-4ae8-aee7-5e0ad394b426_zpsc8ba4baa.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>This is by far one of the best books I have read this year. It’s one of those books... 5 stars is just not enough! It was emotional, moving, powerful, and just all around a great read. The writing was fantastic. It has love/romance, some violence, suspense, it’s a dark read, but it also had some moments that were completely heartwarming. I would recommend this to anyone who enjoyed ‘The Hunger Games’, but personally, I feel that this was MUCH BETTER than ‘The Hunger Games.’ I can’t believe this is a debut novel. Lexi and Cole’s story touched my heart. The next book can’t come out soon enough. This book is to be released on June 28th, 2013 and I would recommend EVERYONE pick it up and read it! It was <b>that good!</b><br><br><br><br><i>**ARC provided by authors via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review**</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="12082405920309928401" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/593250291" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/593250291?book_show_action=true">Apr 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=2013-release">2013-release</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer593250291" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16608188067583957170"><b>✰★✰ 4.5 STARS. ✰★✰</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418052i/827474.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"To the outside, I'm filth now. I'll never be allowed to return to the life I knew. No one ever does."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><b>Branded</b> tells the story of a young girl named Lexi Hamilton. In a future world, the world as it is after World War V, all,the power is in the hands of a cruel, sadistic leader, aka The Commander. People who commit one of the seven deadly sins are branded according to the sin they've commited and exiled to The Hole. A horrible place where there's no form of luxury an</span>
  <span id="freeText16608188067583957170" style="display:none"><b>✰★✰ 4.5 STARS. ✰★✰</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418052i/827474.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"To the outside, I'm filth now. I'll never be allowed to return to the life I knew. No one ever does."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>Branded</b> tells the story of a young girl named Lexi Hamilton. In a future world, the world as it is after World War V, all,the power is in the hands of a cruel, sadistic leader, aka The Commander. People who commit one of the seven deadly sins are branded according to the sin they've commited and exiled to The Hole. A horrible place where there's no form of luxury and barely a scratch of humanity left. There the "Sinners" have to work under the command of their powerful leader. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Now LUST wraps around my neck like blue fingers strangling me. I've been accused of a crime I didn't commit and now the Hole is my new home."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418052i/827475.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As soon as Lexi arrives at the Hole she is assigned her own, personal guard <b>Cole.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418052i/827476._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>His job is to make sure she follows the Commander's orders, gets at work on time every day and that she doesn't cause any trouble. Even though Cole technically works for Lexi's number one enemy, he seems different than most of the other guards. He's kinder, more understanding and doesn't treat her like the sinner she's made out to be. Slowly but surely, Lexi and Cole grow closer but they both know relationships betweens sinners and their guard are strictly forbidden. So, they try to keep their distance as much as possible. <br><br>In the meantime, Lexi tries to adjust to the harsh new reality of the hell hole she now lives in. And even though, the Commander has taken away her free choice and personal belongings, she's determined not to let him crush her spirit and soul.<br><br><b>
  <i>"I was abandoned, neglected, starved, betrayed and abused. I've already been treated like the scum of the earth, so the Hole is nothing new. He wants to erase every sign of my existence on this earth, but I won't let that happen. He can strip me naked, but he'll never reach my soul. It's personal, completely personal."</i>
</b><br><br>All she wants is to be free again...<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418052i/827477.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And therefore, she's willing to fight, fight the corrupt system that puts innocent people away, treats them like they're less worthy and disrobes them of their humanity. Together with the few people she can trust, she tries to make to best of her new living situations, all the while remembering her fathers mantra:<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    "You can overcome anything...short of death."
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>And while the living conditions in the Hole aren't all that great, some of the people and even a certain hilarious and loyal dog named Zeus, living there, more than make up for it (although there are plenty of others that try to make Lexi's life even more miserable). <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397390i/766764.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Everything about you sucks me in. No matter how hard I try to hate you or be disgusted, the opposite happens. You're like my magnet. You pull me in, but when I get to close it takes everything I have to remain at a safe distantie."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418052i/827478.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At first, when I started reading this story, it remined me a little of the Hunger Games. And since I'm a big fan of that series, I immediatly knew I was going to like it. It had the same intriguing, dystopian vibe but as the story progressed, it turned out to be a so much more than just a Hunger Games-like novel. It had it's own unique storyline and characters that kept me hooked from the start. The last final chapters were nerve-wrecking and emotional but luckily there was <b>NO cliffhanger.</b><br><br>I really enjoyed this captivating, action-filled and, at times, sweet story and would highly recommend it to anyone who's a fan of dystopian novels (and even if you're not a fan of the genre, I'd still recommend it because of the powerful message this story tells, that I think will appeal to many readers). <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Most of all, I wish for peace. If I survive this, all I want is to live with Cole and to live in peace for the rest of my life, knowing I made the right choice."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418052i/827479.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~<br><br><br><i>***ARC courtesy of the authors via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review***</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="16608188067583957170" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_552223044" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/552223044" />
    <a title="Georgia ♥ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9138738-georgia"><img alt="Georgia ♥ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1377186210p2/9138738.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/552223044?book_show_action=true">Mar 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Georgia ♥ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Georgia ♥ " href="/user/show/9138738-georgia">Georgia ♥ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=arc-copy-to-review">arc-copy-to-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=sobbing-mess">sobbing-mess</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=suspense-mystery">suspense-mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=abused-hero-or-and-heroine">abused-hero-or-and-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=favourite-cause-it-is-unique">favourite-cause-it-is-unique</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=tattoos-and-piercing">tattoos-and-piercing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=the-sound-of-my-heart-breaking">the-sound-of-my-heart-breaking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=adventure">adventure</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer552223044" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17842534778931018820"><b>4 Sins & Sinners Stars</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Darkness. Death. Violence. Pain.<br/><br/>Now, everyday is a fight for survival. But I won’t die. I won’t let them win.<br/><br/>The Hole can’t keep me. The Hole can’t break me.<br/>I am more than my brand. I’m a fighter.<br/><br/>My name is Lexi Hamilton, and this is my story.</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410875i/806264._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>In a world ravaged by Wars, a new society has emerged and a madman whose sadistic view of humanity rules the people with an iron fist. The Commander is now in power by murdering anyone that stands in his way. Justice is a thing of </span>
  <span id="freeText17842534778931018820" style="display:none"><b>4 Sins &amp; Sinners Stars</b><br><br><b>
  <i>Darkness. Death. Violence. Pain.<br><br>Now, everyday is a fight for survival. But I won’t die. I won’t let them win.<br><br>The Hole can’t keep me. The Hole can’t break me.<br>I am more than my brand. I’m a fighter.<br><br>My name is Lexi Hamilton, and this is my story.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410875i/806264._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In a world ravaged by Wars, a new society has emerged and a madman whose sadistic view of humanity rules the people with an iron fist. The Commander is now in power by murdering anyone that stands in his way. Justice is a thing of the past and the people are no longer equal. There is the Upper Society and there is the Hole. Where the Sinners are forced to live and die.<br><br><b>
  <i>"I think dying is easier compared to living here.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412067i/810161._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Accused of crimes and actions they might have never committed, branded like animals and imprisoned in the worst prison to kill or be killed, starve and driven insane. Die of a simple infection and beg for a small piece of bread. No respect, no dignity, no future. They were found guilty of the 7 Deadly Sins and this is their penance.<br><br><b>
  <i>Lust ~ Gluttony ~ Greed ~ Sloth ~ Wrath ~ Envy ~ Pride</i>
</b><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412067i/810162._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A young woman on the verge of ending her life, stands on the brink of sanity. Abused and despaired she is sentenced to the hole, a sinner of lust. Forced to her limits, she will either break or she will find deep in the darkest places of her soul, the power to fight back and make a stand for herself, her late a father, a small child and love, that is found in the least possible places.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Be strong for the times ahead. Stand up for those who cannot. And remember, you can overcome anything short of death."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412067i/810163._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Lexi &amp; Cole</b>, a Sinner and a Guard, two young people will rise above themselves. They will sacrifice everything and through blood and tears, they will try to set the world free. Hoping that they will manage to survive the battle and finally will be allowed to be together.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Without you, I’m already dead, and each day I get to be with you is one more day we didn’t have yesterday."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410875i/806262._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Gritty, emotional, intense, heartbreaking and ultimately thought-provoking, this book gripped me from the first word and never let me go. Suspenseful and hopelessly romantic, brutally honest and almost angry, a highly recommended story not only for dystopian fans but for all book lovers. The authors pull no punches. Feelings and ugly truths are not implied but laid bare before your eyes, engaging all your senses. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380412067ra/810164.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Strong writing, believable characters, amazing world building and a forbidden love that transcends its physical limitations and is expressed by a stolen glance and hidden caress.<br><br>Kudos for a book well-done! <br><br><b><i>**ARC courtesy of Victory Editing via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review**</i><br><br>Thank you for an amazing read! Can't wait for the next... More Lexi, Cole, Sin &amp; Sinners, Fighters and Philosophers and a world that needs to stand up against injustice.</b><br><br>I NEED THE 2nd BOOK!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380376360ra/731164.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>*Pre-ARC thoughts and feelings:</i><br><br><b>Oooh...</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397206ra/766207.gif" width="500" height="287" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>Best blurb nomination!!!</i>
</b><br></span>

<div id="review_616888604" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/616888604" />
    <a title="Paula " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2879703-paula"><img alt="Paula " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1536687412p2/2879703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/616888604?book_show_action=true">May 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Paula " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Paula " href="/user/show/2879703-paula">Paula </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2879703-paula?shelf=dystopian-fiction">dystopian-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2879703-paula?shelf=new-adult-romance">new-adult-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer616888604" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5306262680624300658"><br/>With its very original dystopian setting and fascinating storyline, I had hoped <i>Branded</i> would be better than it turned out. Unfortunately, this story did not work for me. <br/><br/>Lexi Hamilton has been branded a sinner for all to see around her neck. Lust is her sin, even though she is innocent of her crime. She’s been sent to the Hole, where all the sinners go to live the rest of their lives. The Hole has now become Lexi’s own personal hell and home. The Commander created the Hole when he came into pow</span>
  <span id="freeText5306262680624300658" style="display:none"><br />With its very original dystopian setting and fascinating storyline, I had hoped <i>Branded</i> would be better than it turned out. Unfortunately, this story did not work for me. <br /><br />Lexi Hamilton has been branded a sinner for all to see around her neck. Lust is her sin, even though she is innocent of her crime. She’s been sent to the Hole, where all the sinners go to live the rest of their lives. The Hole has now become Lexi’s own personal hell and home. The Commander created the Hole when he came into power fifty years ago. In his crazy mind, he thinks the seven deadly sins are to blame for the downfall of society. So, once a person is accused of one of the sins, there is no judge or jury, the final judgment is guilt. The Hole is a dirty, ugly, and violent place where the sinners must work the job they’re assigned or be punished. Most of the sinners have lost their humanity over time in a harsh world where it takes smarts and strength to survive.<br /><br />Lexi was assigned to a guard named Cole the moment she arrived. Cole is not like the rest of the guards, who can be just as terrifying and dangerous as the sinners. Something about him is good. He hasn’t been tainted by the Hole yet and still believes in humanity. But he’s still been led astray by the Commander, judging the sinners by the brand they wear. The more he’s around Lexi, the more he starts to see her as an innocent person and not someone whose been branded as a whore. And the more time they spend together, the closer they grow. Eventually they confess their feelings for one another, even though they know it's forbidden. And, if found out, they would be tortured and killed. This doesn’t stop them from falling for each other. But in order to be together, they must survive the Hole and fight for their freedom.<br /><br />Sounds pretty darn good right? And, it does start out good. I was enthralled and excited, at first. But by the second half of the story (or sooner), that's when the story fell apart.<br /><br />One of the main issues I had with this story is that the romance happened too fast. The feelings were rushed. The authors could’ve convinced me that these two fell in love so quickly if there was better build up and development. Instead, it was a bad case of insta-love. Falling in love quickly can work, if it’s well written. This is a dreaded case of "telling not showing." I wanted to understand and feel what they were feeling, but I never felt impacted by this forbidden relationship.<br /><br />My next issue is the character development. It wasn't consistent. Everything changed once they confessed their affections to each other. I didn’t feel like I was reading the same characters anymore, especially with Cole. I thought Cole turned into a pathetic love sick puppy, and Lexi was leading him around by a leash. I was completely appalled by how much Cole tolerated from Lexi. I wanted the tough and strong Cole back that I met in the beginning. And, while Lexi kept trying to remain strong during the story, which is admirable because of everything she’s endured, her actions contradicted her words. She came across as weak and immature, especially when she didn't stand up for herself when she had the chance to show how strong she really is. I didn't feel like there was much character growth with her. <br /><br />The pacing slowed down for me by the second half, then the ending felt rushed and unbelievable. The dialogue was immature and there were a lot of details about the story that felt unrealistic and were explained badly. I almost gave up but I kept reading with the hopes the story would get better. It never did and left me feeling frustrated and annoyed. I've decided not to continue the series. <br /><br />Rating: D+<br />Heat: Sweet<br /><br /><br />-- <i>A <a href="http://romanticbookaffairs.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Romantic Book Affairs</a> Review</i><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Find us on <a href="https://twitter.com/rombookaffairs" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> and <a href="http://facebook.com/rombookaffairs" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> too!</i>
</b> <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5306262680624300658" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_595045829" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/595045829" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/595045829?book_show_action=true">Apr 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=arc-copy-net-galley">arc-copy-net-galley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=june-reads">june-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer595045829" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer626518263997276661"> "You Can Over Come Anything <br/> Short of Death"<br/><br/>Abi Ketner and Missy Kalicicki have written a brilliant Dystopian story that takes the reader on a journey that is terrifying, gruesome, violent, and heartwrenching. Through all of this horror and heartache, there is a love that grows between a guard and a "Sinner and the odds are stacked against them. Can love survive in a world that knows very little peace, or will it fizzle away in the midst of all the chaos.<br/>This story captured my attention from th</span>
  <span id="freeText626518263997276661" style="display:none"> "You Can Over Come Anything <br /> Short of Death"<br /><br />Abi Ketner and Missy Kalicicki have written a brilliant Dystopian story that takes the reader on a journey that is terrifying, gruesome, violent, and heartwrenching. Through all of this horror and heartache, there is a love that grows between a guard and a "Sinner and the odds are stacked against them. Can love survive in a world that knows very little peace, or will it fizzle away in the midst of all the chaos.<br />This story captured my attention from the first page, all the way through to the very last. At times it was so hard to read through all of the suffering that took place in "The Hole", but there was a nice balance between the violence and the love of Lexi and Cole. Another wonderful addition and ray of sunlight was the guard dog, Zeus. That dog was impossible not to love, and he added humor to a somewhat somber story.<br /><br />The story takes place in "The Hole." This is a place that is surrounded by twenty foot cement walls and is basically a prison with no rules. The people that are sent there have supposedly broke some kind of laws in "high society" and they are called "The Sinners." They do not get a court hearing,and once they are taken into the Hole they will never come out. The Hole is run by the Commander; and interestingly enough his identity is not known to anyone. He has a firm belief that there is no forgiveness for the sinners, and he rules with a steel fist which no one wants to cross. The guards that work for him, are ones that no one is allowed to befriend, and the penalty of falling in love with one is a gruesome death. <br />The sinner becomes "Branded" with a metal collar that tightens and burns there skin with the sin they are being accused of. ( Blue-Lust; Orange-Gluttony; Yellow-Greed; Black-Sloth; Red-Wrath; Green-Envy; Purple-Pride.)<br />Lexi Hamilton is branded with Blue (for lust) and her guard is a young man named Cole. These two live in close quarters, and he also takes her to and from the hospital each day where Lexi has to work. These two end up very close, and the bond that they share becomes stronger as they begin to trust one another. Lexi has endured unimaginable events in her lifetime, and Cole eventually becomes extremely protective of her. In the midst of war and violence their love blossoms, and is a beautiful reminder of what a person might want to live for. This is eventually what drives them to survive in this destructive place, and to strive for something better in the future.<br />Along the way, other friendships are formed, and huge revelations as well. There is just so much going on in this story, that there is never a dull moment. In fact, there are secrets that continue to be revealed right up until the very end.<br />If I could rate higher than five stars, I would. There was a point in the story where I actually had goose bumps with what was happening. I laughed, I cried, and I was surprised, this book was an incredible journey of what a person will endure in the name of survival. Also, no matter how hopeless a situation may seem, there is always hope that things can and will get better. <br />The writing from the authors is top quality and they have made a new fan with me. I will for sure be following their stories in the future, as I feel they have an extremely successful career ahead of them if they keep writing the way they did with this book.<br /><br />Thank you to the authors and net galley for providing me with the ARC for this book in exchange for an honest review.</span>
  <a data-text-id="626518263997276661" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText11365937709320723264" style="display:none">I read this because Abookutopia channel recommended it and I'll tell you I'm not dissapointed.<br><br>Cole and Lexi are great together and you'll love Zeus, best pet character ever!<br><br>Update: There will be a harcover edition and I can't wait for it.<br><br>The concept is great, the romance is great, and I thought this was a little bit more adult than other YA dystopians. <div id="review_613840767" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="destini mia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia"><img alt="destini mia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499903277p2/13742215.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/613840767?book_show_action=true">May 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="destini mia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="destini mia" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia">destini mia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13742215-destini-mia?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13742215-destini-mia?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer613840767" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11951012452858424382"><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> Never did I imagine they’d come for me. Never did I imagine all those nights I heard them dragging someone else away that I’d join them.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416851ra/823768.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Casting:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421349i/836884._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410875i/806264._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>Branded</i> was fast paced, raw and gritty, with a heart wrenching romance and a captivating story. One of my absolute favorites of this year!<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421349i/836885.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>It’s post WWV, where the privileged live in fear of being accused and the unlucky one’s fight for their life in the Hole. <br/>With a twisted, unyielding Commander as their leader, those who oppose him are murd</span>
  <span id="freeText11951012452858424382" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> Never did I imagine they’d come for me. Never did I imagine all those nights I heard them dragging someone else away that I’d join them.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416851ra/823768.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Casting:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421349i/836884._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410875i/806264._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Branded</i> was fast paced, raw and gritty, with a heart wrenching romance and a captivating story. One of my absolute favorites of this year!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421349i/836885.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>It’s post WWV, where the privileged live in fear of being accused and the unlucky one’s fight for their life in the Hole. <br>With a twisted, unyielding Commander as their leader, those who oppose him are murdered and the sinners are sent to the Hole where they can be contained. <br><i>
  <blockquote> He controls our depraved society and believes sinners make the human race unforgivable. His power is a crushing fist, rendering all beneath him helpless. So much so, even family members turn on each other when an accusation surfaces. Just an accusation. No trial, no evidence, nothing but an accusation.</blockquote>
</i><br>Lexi has been accused so, she is sent to the Hole with LUST wrapped around her neck. In the Hole she finds violence, rapes, and death awaiting her but she’s stronger than all that. She’s a survivor. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> He thinks he can destroy me by stripping away my possessions. But he can’t and I won’t let them take my memories, my ambition, and my pride. </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421349i/836886.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I have a soft stop for Dystopian books but <i>Branded</i> completely exceeded my expectations. There was a forbidden romance that had my stomach in knots (and I mean <b>forbidden</b>, like Eve eating the apple <b>forbidden</b>) and a wonderful storyline.<br><i>
  <blockquote> They’re chosen from a young age and trained in combat. They kept order of society by using violent methods of intimidation. No one befriends a guard. Relationships with them are forbidden inside the Hole.</blockquote>
</i><br>But even with the romance, there was an actual <i>story</i> too. I loved that I was equally enthralled with the romance as I was with the storyline. There were twists and turns I didn’t see coming and I was kept at the edge of my seat the whole time.<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> He can strip me naked, but he’ll never reach my soul. </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421349i/836887._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Lexi is one of the strongest, most courageous characters I've read about and definitely makes it to my favorites. I’m pretty sure I have a girl crush on her, that’s how much I liked her. I loved her drive and determination, her ability to help others, and the way she held on to her humanity in one of the darkest places.<br><i>
  <blockquote> Every day, I witness the ugliness of humanity and it diminishes my faith in the goodness of people.</blockquote>
</i><br>And then there was Cole, who had me stuck in a permanent swoon. <br><i>
  <blockquote> “I’ll fight for us because nothing else brings me joy except loving you,” he whispers in my ear.</blockquote>
</i><br>Holy hotness, <b>that man has my heart, body, and soul.</b> Right from the beginning you could tell he was different. <br><i>
  <blockquote> “The last thing I want is for you to be afraid of me. But I want you to trust me. I need you to trust me.”<br>“Why?”<br>“I don’t know why and it scares the hell out of me.”</blockquote>
</i><br>He wasn’t as mean, cold, wraped and absolutely repulsive as the other guards. You could see that he had a heart. <br><i>
  <blockquote> “Just leave me,” I whisper into his ear.<br>“Never.”</blockquote>
</i><br><b>Even with it being forbidden, Cole and Lexi’s relationship was beautiful.</b> Not everything was filled with death and despair and they were able to escape into each other, whether it was with some <b>steamy</b> lip locking or bantering around. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421349ra/836888.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “I love you,” I say. <br>He’s breathing faster, leaning into me, kissing my forehead, my temples, and my cheeks. He runs his lips down to my ear and whispers. “I love you too.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421349i/836889.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I understand that this story isn’t for everybody because, despite it being YA, there were some gritty, dark, and gruesome scenes that had me cringing. <br>However, I would definitely recommend this to anyone who wants and steamy romance, unpredictable turns, and an action packed story. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> Be strong for the times ahead. Stand up for those who cannot. And remember, you can overcome anything short of death.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br><i>**ARC courtesy of Victory Editing via NetGalley in exchange for a honest review**</i></span>

<div id="review_595243059" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/595243059" />
    <a title="Brenna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12928663-brenna"><img alt="Brenna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580475762p2/12928663.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/595243059?book_show_action=true">Apr 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brenna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brenna" href="/user/show/12928663-brenna">Brenna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=action-suspense-crime">action-suspense-crime</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=drove-me-crazy">drove-me-crazy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer595243059" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13780859662707733659"><b>2 1/2 stars </b><br/><br/><b>I have so many conflicting feelings about this. On one hand, I love the concept and it was an easy book to get through. On the other, I couldn’t stop thinking about things that bothered me that took away from the overall enjoyment of the book.</b><br/><br/>It all begins with Lexi Hamilton; she has just been branded a sinner. She now wears a blue brand signifying her alleged sin of lust on her neck. In her world, anyone who is accused of one of the seven deadly sins is sent to the Hole. There is no</span>
  <span id="freeText13780859662707733659" style="display:none"><b>2 1/2 stars </b><br /><br /><b>I have so many conflicting feelings about this. On one hand, I love the concept and it was an easy book to get through. On the other, I couldn’t stop thinking about things that bothered me that took away from the overall enjoyment of the book.</b><br /><br />It all begins with Lexi Hamilton; she has just been branded a sinner. She now wears a blue brand signifying her alleged sin of lust on her neck. In her world, anyone who is accused of one of the seven deadly sins is sent to the Hole. There is no trial, no ‘innocent until proven guilty’; an accusation is all it takes. Sinners are assigned jobs and live on whatever they make from that task. Corruption, poverty and crime run rampant among sinners and guards of the Hole. <br /><i>
  <blockquote>To the outside, I’m filth now. I’ll never be allowed to return to the life I knew. No one ever does.</blockquote>
</i><br />Once Lexi arrives at the Hole, she is assigned a job at the hospital and also given a guard. Cole lives in a room connected to hers, escorts her to and from work, and protects her from other sinners (and guards). Due to the color of Lexi’s brand, that makes her a huge target. <br /><i>
  <blockquote> “Skank! We know you’re in there,” says a screechy voice. <br />“Slut! Open the door,” says a second voice. <br />“We’ve been dreaming about touching you all night… We promise to be gentle.” They laugh. </blockquote>
</i><br />Not long passes before lines become blurred between Cole and Lexi. It is strictly forbidden for guards and sinners to be together and have a relationship. It is a crime punishable by death. Instead of treating Lexi like a whore or servant like many of the other corrupt guards in the Hole, Cole treats Lexi with respect. He protects her, doesn’t take advantage of her, and even helps her when asked. These are things that look very bad in the eyes of the Commander. <br /><i>
  <blockquote> “The last thing I want is for you to be afraid of me. But I want you to trust me. I need you to trust me.” He sighs and I hear the pain and confusion in his voice. <br />“Why?” <br />“I don’t know why and it scares the hell out of me.” He swallows hard and then scratches the back of his head while biting his lower lip. Part of me screams for him to run for his own safety, yet I don’t want him to move. My heart begs… Please stay with me. Forever. <br />“I hate when you leave, and that scares me too.”</blockquote>
</i><br />Their feelings for each other progress very quickly and it’s not long before they are completely lost to one another. <br /><i>
  <blockquote> “There’s nothing I can do to change who I am, what I’ve been labeled.” <br />“You’re amazing just the way you are. There’s not a single thing I would change about you. When you smile my entire world stops. All I see is you. I need you.” My head shakes back and forth, willing his words away. If he keeps this up, I don’t know if my promise to Sutton will stick. <br />“No, you don’t. You have to stop.” <br />“I wish I knew how.” </blockquote>
</i><br />I had a real issue taking Cole and Lexi seriously together. I really thought I was going to love Cole as a character. I wanted to learn more about him, but that never happens. Here’s what I can tell you about Cole now that I’ve finished this book… He’s hot, he is a good guard, he has a dog (who’s pretty awesome – love Zeus!), and he loves Lexi. That just isn’t enough for me. He seemed tough and fair, but I wanted him to have more depth. Where is the development? What is his story? He just suddenly shifts to this almost lovesick puppy dog. I’m all for swoon, but it just didn’t feel right. It wasn’t realistic for things to happen as quickly as they did and I couldn’t tell why they were in love with each other. This was definitely a case of telling versus showing. Then the cheesy dialogue... I just couldn’t take it seriously anymore.<br /><i>
  <blockquote> But I can’t deny how I feel toward Cole. Nothing and no one could ever compare to him. All I can think about are his honest brown eyes, the scar on his lip, and the intense expression when he kisses me that <b>sucks me in like a vacuum</b>. I feel drunk on him—just crazy about his face, his hands, and his body. Too crazy.<br />…<br /> “Babe, let’s take it slow. I don’t want to move too fast…<b> I don’t just want to make love. I want to make our love last.</b>” </blockquote>
</i> <br /><i>
  <b>Seriously?!</b>
</i> Way to quote a country singer there Cole. I honestly was thinking that was going to be a cute, silly moment where they were going to tease each other or something. But nope. Totally serious. O.o<br /><br />Lexi as a heroine was confounding and often times just plain irritating. I have to admit that she’s a strong girl, and by that I mean, she’s still <i>living</i> after all she has endured in her life (both inside and outside of the Hole). She just did not work as a narrator though; she is constantly saying how strong she is, but then acting the complete opposite way. Her constant crying, tantrums, throwing up (lol), and cheesy inner monologues about Cole got to be so often that I just couldn’t <i>feel</i> for her like I wanted. And I trust me, I really did want to, what she goes through is AWFUL, some of the worst things imaginable. Yet, I just didn't like her. Her transformation throughout the book also felt inconsistent and her decisions sometimes made me want to slap some sense into her. <br /><br />After finishing this, I am just so confused. I kind of feel like... <b>What am I missing? What am I not seeing that everyone else did?</b> I wanted so badly to love this one and was so excited about it. I still think the concept is awesome and really intriguing, ultimately though the writing was chopping and the dialogue juvenile at times. I just think more time needed to be spent on the development of the characters, their relationships, and even on building the world. The last 10-15% of this book I really think should have been in the second. I loved the twists, but then things ended up feeling too easy. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I cannot believe the commander was killed just like that. It was so anticlimactic. That should have been a HUGE moment, with more build up. You find out that he's Sutton's brother, then BAM - he's her stepdad, then a minute later he's dead. It would have been SO much more interesting if that had been developed more and maybe gone into the next book. Just too easy. Yeah, he says his guards will come after them, but who really cares about them? Everything is built around the power of the Commander the whole book, then it's done, just like that. No bueno. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> While there are loose threads, it ends at a point where I would feel fine with ending it there and not having another book. Even with my complaints, I didn’t have a hard time getting through this book. It goes by pretty fast and there was enough going on to keep my attention, just maybe with some eye rolling along the way… <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13780859662707733659" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1429795008" />
