  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1429795008?book_show_action=true">Oct 31, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Reynita Maharani ★ The Night Reader ★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Reynita Maharani ★ The Night Reader ★" href="/user/show/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader">Reynita Maharani ★ The Night Reader ★</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=i-give-up">i-give-up</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=made-me-want-to-slap-the-heroine">made-me-want-to-slap-the-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=didn-t-live-up-my-expectations">didn-t-live-up-my-expectations</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=new-adult-books">new-adult-books</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1429795008" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6592117126270858982">DNF @ 20%<br/><br/>before I start reviewing this book I want to say thank to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/31006810-veronica' rel='nofollow noopener'>my kind friend Veronica </a> who answered my question about this book, but I'm sorry to let you down :( <br/><br/>There are seven deadly sins :<br/>Pride > Purple Envy > Green <br/>Wrath > Red Sloth > Black<br/>Greed >Yellow Lust > Blue <br/>Gluttony > Orange <br/><br/>if you are accused then you will be brought to The Hole, where all the sinners live and where you will be branded by the color of your sin on your neck.<br/>All of the sinners have a job and every sinners have a </span>
  <span id="freeText6592117126270858982" style="display:none">DNF @ 20%<br><br>before I start reviewing this book I want to say thank to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/31006810-veronica" rel="nofollow noopener">my kind friend Veronica </a> who answered my question about this book, but I'm sorry to let you down :( <br><br>There are seven deadly sins :<br>Pride &gt; Purple Envy &gt; Green <br>Wrath &gt; Red Sloth &gt; Black<br>Greed &gt;Yellow Lust &gt; Blue <br>Gluttony &gt; Orange <br><br>if you are accused then you will be brought to The Hole, where all the sinners live and where you will be branded by the color of your sin on your neck.<br>All of the sinners have a job and every sinners have a guard. The guards responsibilty are to make sure the sinners they guarded are alive and to escort them to go to work and to their rooms after working.<br><br>Why did I give up ?<br>Ok here's the reason : <br>I don't want to spoil anything about this book to you but maybe I'm just gonna give a very light spoiler.<br>when Lexi (our Heroine) goes back from working, there is something happen with Lexi and Cole (our Hero). So Lexi and Cole have to run to save their lifes. but when Lexi runs her ankle gets twisted or something so she just stops running and sit on the ground while their enemies chasing them. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397501158ra/9284159.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I was like " are you serious!?!?!?! I know your ankle is twisted but at least run for your life don't just do that!" <br>then Cole have to carry her, But when they climb up a fence, surprisingly she can climbs too and she can walks again.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1463414828ra/19116121.gif" width="340" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>this book is my first New Adult book and I've waited to read it for months and I had a very high expectation but I didn't get what I wanted and I just couldn't continue reading it anymore.<br>So, guys if you have any recommendations about Dark romance (not erotica) NA books, don't hesitate to tell me because I'd love to get recommendations about NA books :D <br><br>Thank you for reading my short review!! Have A great day!!<br>P.S. Thanks again, Veronica!!<br> <br><br><br><br> <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6592117126270858982" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_683134493" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/683134493" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/683134493?book_show_action=true">Aug 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=oops-let-s-do-it-again-romance">oops-let-s-do-it-again-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=third-time-s-the-charm-romance">third-time-s-the-charm-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=young-adult-ness">young-adult-ness</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=new-adult-express">new-adult-express</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=read-to-review">read-to-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=i-trust-my-friends">i-trust-my-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer683134493" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18243507537852641518"><b>2.5-3 stars!</b><br/><br/><i>Note: The book has recently been updated with a new cover and has brand new chapters (extra 70 pages).</i><br/><br/>When I first read this book last summer, I thought it was flawless – I especially loved that the story gave me a total escapism feeling. As time goes by, I’ve noticed that my tastes change (like a lot) and I become more jaded & critical. I just want to point out that this review is not very trustworthy – the first time reading I gave this book 5 stars. Now almost a year later it bare</span>
  <span id="freeText18243507537852641518" style="display:none"><b>2.5-3 stars!</b><br><br><i>Note: The book has recently been updated with a new cover and has brand new chapters (extra 70 pages).</i><br><br>When I first read this book last summer, I thought it was flawless – I especially loved that the story gave me a total escapism feeling. As time goes by, I’ve noticed that my tastes change (like a lot) and I become more jaded &amp; critical. I just want to point out that this review is not very trustworthy – the first time reading I gave this book 5 stars. Now almost a year later it barely scrapes a satisfactory rating. This is going to sound harsh but I personally didn’t see the difference between the old version and the updated one I just finished reading. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400369036i/9667967._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lexi lives in a dystopian world where everything is governed by the Commander, and if accused of one of the seven deadly sins, that person is immediately thrown into the Hole, a wretched, cursed place where slave labor and worse basically happen. In Lexi’s unfortunate case, she was wrongfully accused of <i>lust,</i> one of the worst sins to be branded with, and is assigned to Cole, the hero of the book and Lexi’s new guard. <br><br>Cole becomes Lexi’s guard and has orders to protect her – according to Lexi and others he has a very appealing physical form and is the best of the best out of all the guards. The only crime worse than being branded with one of the seven sins is for a Guard to fall in love with a Sinner, and that is precisely what happens in this story.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400369036i/9667968.jpg" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Before I get all critical, I do want to point out that it’s tough to balance both dystopian and romance. Those two themes shouldn’t even be in the same sentence as they’re polar opposites so I do applaud the authors for being daring and bold. <br><br>For me though, this book weighed more on the romance side than dystopian, and I felt like a lot of the character interactions were childish, unbelievable, or annoying. <br><br>- From the start I had this feeling like there were exceptions made for Lexi: she just <i>had</i> to get the nice and hot guard Cole, she just <i>had</i> to meet the kind Dr. Sutton, she just <i>had</i> to be instrumental in the revolt, etc…I mean this is freaking dystopian society we’re talking about here! I need to <i>feel</i> like Lexi is just like any other branded Sinner not just some girl who got an easy pass because she’s the heroine and deserves an HEA. <br>- Cole is a guard? Aside from the uniform, you could’ve fooled me. The VERY first moment he sees her he gives her a <i>“pained look.”</i> Why is he, a GUARD, sympathizing with her??? And on first sight too? This guy is just too good to be true and in any other setting (like contemporary for instance) I would’ve adored him. Truly, I would’ve but since this isn’t, at least try to make his character convincing before he falls for Lexi!<br><br>I feel myself getting ranty now so I’m going to stop because it makes me sad that a book I adored last year ends up receiving a rant this year. The book premise is awesome, but the writing felt a little immature and as for the story, well...suffice it to say I liked it but didn’t love it – a very bumpy ride. <br><br><i>Copy provided by the authors via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.</i><br></span>

<div id="review_640328370" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/640328370" />
    <a title="Lucia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia"><img alt="Lucia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484242793p2/8837962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/640328370?book_show_action=true">Jun 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucia" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia">Lucia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Lucia by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=dystopia">dystopia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=1-2-stars-read">1-2-stars-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer640328370" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer110949273014273186"><b>I liked the emotional first half of the book. But after promising introduction into this story I was a little bit disappointed with the second half which lacked element of surprise or twists that would keep me on my toes.</b><br/>My Lexi and Cole:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425228i/848432._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>In Branded, after World War V, country is ruled by Commander who sends all "sinners" into The Hole as a way of keeping society "pure". All sinners are guarded by Guards of Commander and relationship of any form between sinner and guard is strictly forbidden. The</i></span>
  <span id="freeText110949273014273186" style="display:none"><b>I liked the emotional first half of the book. But after promising introduction into this story I was a little bit disappointed with the second half which lacked element of surprise or twists that would keep me on my toes.</b><br>My Lexi and Cole:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425228i/848432._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>In Branded, after World War V, country is ruled by Commander who sends all "sinners" into The Hole as a way of keeping society "pure". All sinners are guarded by Guards of Commander and relationship of any form between sinner and guard is strictly forbidden. There is no trial, no evidence gathering. Accused sinners are sent to the Hole right away. And that is exactly the case of Lexi Hamilton - accused of sin, branded with sign symbolising a sin she supposedly committed and sent to the Hole with no real chance for survival. Her only chance may be Cole, the guard assigned to watch her. Byt why and for what cost?</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425228i/848433._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Cole</b> was a tough guy. Strong, fearless, focused, well-trained and loyal. Brought up as a guard, he did not have much choice how to live his life but he always tried to make the best out of it. When I got to know him better through out the book, I was completely enraptured by his character. If I was judging this book based on Cole, I would rate it with 5 stars because he deserves all stars in the world. Yeah, he was that awesome!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425228i/848434._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Lexi</b>'s life was turned up side down. Living in unhuman conditions, witnessing terrible things and being on her own unable to protect herself in the most dangerouns place on earth. Yeah, her life was not ideal at all and she was very weak. But she never lost hope for better life and always kept going no matter what. <br><blockquote>
  <b>"You can overcome anything...shorth of death.</b>
</blockquote> <br>Branded is about the will to keep fighting for the good cause, about need to survive and maintain some sort of humanity at the same time. The beginning of this book was very <b>emotional</b> for me. It deals with various human's destinies and none of them is easy or overjoyed. <br><br>Unfortunatelly, I had a big <b>problem with characters development</b>. Their feelings evolved and changed rapidly without proper background information or building up. The change came all of the sudden and it left me confused on more than one occasion. Moreover, <b>Lexi was very weak character</b>. She transformed from admirable person to girl who was unable to stand up for herself. I know she had to endure pretty horrible stuff but she was feisty when it came to strangers but when it came to her feeling, she was weak and it annoyed me a lot. And I am not even going to talk about many unbelievable and <b>unrealistic details</b> that kind of frustrated me through out the whole book. <br><br>The blurb of this book immediatelly caught my attention, so when I received a review copy I did not hesitate to dive into it. I really liked the world authors created in this book. But after captivating start, the ending was rushed and left me a little bit bitter and indiferrent...<br><br><i>*ARC received via Netgalley as an exchange for honest review*</i><br><br>MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Reading Is My Breathing</b>
</a></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_678677344" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/678677344" />
    <a title="Lauren" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7864935-lauren"><img alt="Lauren" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1427665068p2/7864935.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/678677344?book_show_action=true">Jul 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lauren" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lauren" href="/user/show/7864935-lauren">Lauren</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7864935-lauren?shelf=this-is-not-how-you-book">this-is-not-how-you-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7864935-lauren?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7864935-lauren?shelf=interiority-complex">interiority-complex</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer678677344" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8196686845867614572"><p>Dear readers, I did not like <i>Branded</i> by Abi Ketner and Missy Kalicicki. Not in the least. When I first read the book blurb, I got excited. A dystopian novel set in an ultra-religious society where people are imprisoned for violating the seven deadly sins, a main character falsely accused and imprisoned for lust, a conflicted guard mysteriously assigned to keep her alive at all costs, and a smidge of star-crossed love thrown in to boot. Sounds great, sign me up! Turns out my initial excitement wa</p></span>
  <span id="freeText8196686845867614572" style="display:none"><p>Dear readers, I did not like <i>Branded</i> by Abi Ketner and Missy Kalicicki. Not in the least. When I first read the book blurb, I got excited. A dystopian novel set in an ultra-religious society where people are imprisoned for violating the seven deadly sins, a main character falsely accused and imprisoned for lust, a conflicted guard mysteriously assigned to keep her alive at all costs, and a smidge of star-crossed love thrown in to boot. Sounds great, sign me up! Turns out my initial excitement was completely unfounded.</p> <p>First off, the authors barely scratch the surface of this dystopian society at all. The world-building outside of the prison for sinners, known as the Hole, was nonexistent. Even the world-building of the Hole itself was only bare-bones minimum. No explanation for why the seven deadly sins replaced the rule of law or what role religion plays in society, no reasons given for the Hole operating in the convoluted way that it does. I could go on, but for the sake of both your precious time and mine, I won’t.</p> <p>The dialogue felt unrealistic and best, and like speechifying at worst. Every so often there was a sentence so nonsensical that it would rip me out of the story and make me stare at the page in bewilderment. On top of this, none of the characters rang true. Not even the dog. The characterization was either one-dimensional or inconsistent. The authors sacrificed any sort of interiority in favor of plot and/or romance. (It was mostly romance).</p> <p>As for any emotions, the authors decided to tell the reader rather than show us any evidence of, well, anything. Lexi says she’s falling in love with Cole. Great! Show me, please. Lexi says the Hole is stripping away her human dignity? How awful! But where’s the evidence? Show me how this is happening!</p> <p>All of the above is forgivable. After all, <i>Branded</i> is a self-published, debut novel. Finishing a novel, no matter what people think of it, is a commendable achievement. I probably would have rated <i>Branded</i> two stars if it were not for one thing that got me completely incensed. You see, people in The Hole are assigned to different jobs. They have no say in their assignment. If they do not show up for their job, they are put to death. One of the jobs assigned to women is that of a prostitute. So we’ve got women being forced into the role of a prostitute - into having sex for money. This is non-consensual sex tantamount to rape. It would be one thing if this idea was explored with some degree of sensitivity, yet these women are all portrayed as sex-hungry sluts. It’s hard for me to believe that two women wrote this into a book.</p> <p>So, do I recommend this book? No. Not in the least. I read it so you, dear readers, don’t have to. One star. ‘F’ for fail. Hopefully I’ll have better luck next time. </p> <p> You can read this review (and others) at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.wrenreads.com">www.wrenreads.com</a></p></span>
  <a data-text-id="8196686845867614572" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer16931952346311986926"><b>BRANDED HAS RUINED ME FROM ALL BOOKS!!!!</b><br/><br/><i>OH. MY. GOD.</i> <br/><br/>That was <b>AMAZING!!!!</b><br/><br/>It was written so well. The story was beautifully constructed throughout the book. There is action, romance and gut-wrenching moments. It was <b>
  <i>one hell of a roller coaster ride</i>
</b>. One I enjoyed so much. There were so <b>many feels</b>. I felt like my heart will leap out of chest and jump into my trembling hands. (My hands weren't trembling mind you but that was how hard the feels where, they were eagerly scrolling down to devour </span>
  <span id="freeText16931952346311986926" style="display:none"><b>BRANDED HAS RUINED ME FROM ALL BOOKS!!!!</b><br /><br /><i>OH. MY. GOD.</i> <br /><br />That was <b>AMAZING!!!!</b><br /><br />It was written so well. The story was beautifully constructed throughout the book. There is action, romance and gut-wrenching moments. It was <b>
  <i>one hell of a roller coaster ride</i>
</b>. One I enjoyed so much. There were so <b>many feels</b>. I felt like my heart will leap out of chest and jump into my trembling hands. (My hands weren't trembling mind you but that was how hard the feels where, they were eagerly scrolling down to devour more words). It was a roller coaster ride that I want to keep waiting in the line for and going back on <b>again and again.</b> I would still be feeling the same as I did when I first read it. <br /><br />Lexi Hamilton has one hell of a story to tell. She has been wrongfully branded for a crime, a sin she didn't commit. I wouldn't wish what happened to her on anyone. It was <b>horrific.</b> <br /><br />I got to read this story pre-edited so when it all done, I will post my favourite quotes. The dialogues, the action and the mystery of what will happen is going to keep you at the edge of your seat until you come to the end and feel numb and wanting for more. There were so many feels that my heart couldn't take more and went <b>numb</b> (I love and devour books like that, this is one book you need to keep your eyes wide open for). <br /><br />It was on hell of a FEEL fest. So when its out this is a book you need to BUY and READ right away! <br /></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_663865878" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/663865878" />
    <a title="Kathryn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22066531-kathryn"><img alt="Kathryn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1462720745p2/22066531.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/663865878?book_show_action=true">Jul 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kathryn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kathryn" href="/user/show/22066531-kathryn">Kathryn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22066531-kathryn?shelf=horrible">horrible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22066531-kathryn?shelf=authors-behaving-badly">authors-behaving-badly</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer663865878&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer663865878" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17654491026091209596"><i>Fifty years ago the Commander came into power and murdered all who opposed him. In his warped mind, the seven deadly sins were the downfall of society. He created the Hole where sinners are branded according to their sins and might survive a few years. At best. <br/>Now LUST wraps around my neck like blue fingers strangling me. I’ve been accused of a crime I didn’t commit and now the Hole is my new home. <br/><br/>Darkness. Death. Violence. Pain. <br/><br/>Now every day is a fight for survival. But I won’t die. I won’t </i></span>
  <span id="freeText17654491026091209596" style="display:none"><i>Fifty years ago the Commander came into power and murdered all who opposed him. In his warped mind, the seven deadly sins were the downfall of society. He created the Hole where sinners are branded according to their sins and might survive a few years. At best. <br />Now LUST wraps around my neck like blue fingers strangling me. I’ve been accused of a crime I didn’t commit and now the Hole is my new home. <br /><br />Darkness. Death. Violence. Pain. <br /><br />Now every day is a fight for survival. But I won’t die. I won’t let them win.<br /><br />The Hole can’t keep me. The Hole can’t break me. <br />I am more than my brand. I’m a fighter. <br />My name is Lexi Hamilton, and this is my story.</i><br /><br />The blurb sounded great and considering it has a four star rating on both Amazon and Goodreads I decided to give it a shot. And at first I believed it was as good as all those reviewers told me it was going to be. The story takes place in a dystopian future where criminals are branded “sinners”, marked with a tattoo (different colors for different sins) and sent to live in a prison/slum like place called the Hole. In the Hole sinners are watched by the guards who regularly abuse and kill them, all with the approval of the Commander who has been running the country as a dictatorship for fifty years. There is no judicial system, no trials, and no ‘innocent until proven guilty’. There is “High Society” where the regular people live and there is the Hole where people accused of the seven deadly sins end up after they are accused.<br /><br />The book starts out with Lexi, a woman from High Society attempting suicide. She fails and is taken into custody by the guards. She is accused of the sin of lust and is branded with a blue band around her neck and sent to the Hole. Once there she is assigned to a Guard named Cole, whose job it is to escort her to work and keep her in line. He has an adjoining room to hers (convenient) and he is the person who explains how the Hole works and what is expected of her as its newest resident.<br /><br />I have to stop here, because seriously, the story gets a bit convoluted and at this point and it will be easier to break down where things start to go wrong for me.<br /><br />1.) The big plot twists in the book are obvious from the get-go and it is written in first person which makes for an awkward and very limited narrative. As readers we only know what Lexi knows, and to be honest it isn’t much.<br /><br />2.) Though the Hole is described as Hell and a basically lawless place where Sinners are abused and executed willy-nilly, Lexi is assigned her own Guard who seems like a nice guy and tells her again and again he has orders to protect her. Huh? She doesn’t question why she has special treatment and that her life is better than all those around her. This got more annoying as the story wore on.<br /><br />3.) It’s pretty obvious from the beginning that Cole and Lexi are destined to fall in love. The problem is that the authors do much more telling than showing in their relationship. I never felt any kind of connection between them other than the characters telling each other how they feel. <br /> <br />4.) Of course love between a Sinner and a Guard is FORBIDDEN. Early in the book Lexi and Cole witness an execution of a couple for this reason. However there are Sinners who are prostitutes and the Guards are allowed to have sex with them. Say what now? So sex for money and favors between the two is okay, but true love is outlawed. And if you fall in love you are executed. What if a Guard fell in love with a prostitute?! I found myself confused over the whole thing.<br /><br />5.) Lexi is assigned to work at the only hospital in the Hole, although she has no medical training whatsoever. It’s okay though, because we don’t ever really find out what she does there anyway, aside from stepping over puddles of puke and folding linens. There are several times I balked at the lack of medical knowledge displayed in this book. <br /><br />6.) Oh the misogyny! This book wouldn’t be complete without the added fun of hating women and women hating on each other. Lexi is branded for the sin of lust even though we know she is innocent. (Of course!) But she has no problem judging other women wearing the same brand and the words slut and whore are thrown around like confetti. Early on in the story Lexi dislikes a nurse named Amber because she flirts with Cole and is later witnesses her in a dark closet with another Guard. She is instantly labeled in Lexi’s mind, without any thought about her motivations or possible victimization. Amber is pretty much a cardboard cutout we are supposed to hate.<br /><br />And let’s not forget that Lexi is innocent of the crime she is accused of! Even though our heroine never proclaims it out loud she thinks it enough that we know it must be true. We get confirmation regarding this later on in the book when Lexi is attacked by several Guards and then is attended to by the doctor who runs the hospital:<br /><br /><blockquote>“I performed a test to make sure you weren’t raped. Cole wasn’t certain if he’d gotten to you in time. Thank God it was negative. You were never raped-but not only will that test reveal a recent sexual encounter, it can report any sexual intercourse that’s happened. It scans the tissues and checks if anything has been stretched, torn, or irritated. It then shows us if you are intact.” He leans over and reaches for my hands. I take a deep breath knowing what’s about to come out of his mouth. “My dear you are a virgin and that’s a medical fact.”</blockquote><br /><br />You see, she IS innocent! And the fetishizing of virginity in romance remains intact. (Okay, not funny. I know.) What we have here, dear reader is an acute case of the Mary Sue. Let’s do a tally, shall we? Lexi has turquoise eyes, is told again and again how beautiful she is by the people around her, she is innocent of the crime of lust and is in fact a virgin, and she is rescued again and again by her hero Cole. Not to mention she has an amazing artistic ability, and ends up being good at everything she attempts, which honestly isn’t much. She’s so self-absorbed that we learn very little about the Hole, the dystopian future that is the setting for this book, or anything else that would have made this story interesting. Not to mention that the doctor has this “scanner” in a hospital that can only afford one bag of morphine!<br /><br />7.) The writing is in this book was okay in the beginning. The fast pace and world building kept my attention for the first few chapters. After that I couldn’t stop rolling my eyes at the horrible dialogue and cardboard characterizations. It did not help that Lexi was either throwing up or crying every other page. I can’t help but think that the authors went out of their way to try and gross us out with their constant description of the smells and sights that Lexi encounters. <br /><br />Here’s a quick breakdown of the bodily fluid mentions:<br />10 vomit<br />8 puke<br />3 throw up<br />51 tears<br />21 cry<br />6 urine<br />75 blood<br /><br />Even the small attempts at humor involve bodily functions and fall flat. Instead of reading a dark thrilling book as promised, I felt like I was reading a gross out and over the top story that pre-teens would share around a campfire. I could continue the list above, but there is little point. The book never gets better, only worse. The premise started out promising but eventually this book sunk into little more than an unrealistic and ridiculous attempt to be the new Hunger Games.<br /><br /><b>My score? D-</b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17654491026091209596" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/645084410" />
    <a title="Catarina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina"><img alt="Catarina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514808293p2/11538033.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/645084410?book_show_action=true">Jun 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catarina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catarina" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina">Catarina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=perfect-book-boyfriend">perfect-book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=dystopia">dystopia</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer645084410" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16358743692939684502"><b>4 Fighting Stars</b><br/><br/>This story takes place in a post-WWV world, which is now a completely different place. <br/>The world is now ruled by the “Commander” and it has to remain pure. <br/>No sins… and no sinners. <br/>The Commander believes that the seven deadly were the cause to the downfall of society and all the sinners that are believed to commit a crime inside one of the seven deadly sins are judged and sent to “The Hole” where a color will identify the type of sin they committed. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425914i/850411.jpg' width='350' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Lexi was sent to the hole and </span>
  <span id="freeText16358743692939684502" style="display:none"><b>4 Fighting Stars</b><br><br>This story takes place in a post-WWV world, which is now a completely different place. <br>The world is now ruled by the “Commander” and it has to remain pure. <br>No sins… and no sinners. <br>The Commander believes that the seven deadly were the cause to the downfall of society and all the sinners that are believed to commit a crime inside one of the seven deadly sins are judged and sent to “The Hole” where a color will identify the type of sin they committed. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425914i/850411.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lexi was sent to the hole and she didn't try to defend herself because she knew it wouldn't matter. There she meets Cole, the guard assigned for her. <br>Relationships between guards and prisoners are strictly forbidden… but Cole starts to see that maybe Lexi isn't so guilty and they can’t help start falling in love. <br>And with that starts a crazy ride. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425914i/850412._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I liked this book. Normally I'm not the biggest fan of dystopian books but this catch my attention and I was not disappointed.<br>There were some things that didn't worked for me, but other than that, it’s a beautiful love story with an original twist and it’s hard not to be hooked to the book and the characters. <br>Definitely a series that I’ll follow. <br><br><i>*ARC courtesy of Victory Editing via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review.*</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="16358743692939684502" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_540623908" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/540623908" />
    <a title="Laurynne Gouws" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10301025-laurynne-gouws"><img alt="Laurynne Gouws" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431101906p2/10301025.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/540623908?book_show_action=true">Feb 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laurynne Gouws" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laurynne Gouws" href="/user/show/10301025-laurynne-gouws">Laurynne Gouws</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10301025-laurynne-gouws?shelf=cbl-book-tours">cbl-book-tours</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10301025-laurynne-gouws?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer540623908" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15328529680324894529"><a href='http://www.cblreviews.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398044i/768794.png' width='400px' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I'd like it to go on record and state that on this day <b>I</b> said <i>"Just you wait and see... Branded is going to become a Bestseller for sure. If this doesn't happen then there's a problem with the system. Injustice will not be tolerated - Branded deserves to be amongst the best."</i><br/><br/>It's been a long time since I read a YA and even longer since I read a dystopian novel. I'd forgotten how much fun they can be. Yes, Branded is YA and considering I'm bordering on 31, I do like more 'risque' books, howev</span>
  <span id="freeText15328529680324894529" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.cblreviews.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398044i/768794.png" width="400px" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I'd like it to go on record and state that on this day <b>I</b> said <i>"Just you wait and see... Branded is going to become a Bestseller for sure. If this doesn't happen then there's a problem with the system. Injustice will not be tolerated - Branded deserves to be amongst the best."</i><br><br>It's been a long time since I read a YA and even longer since I read a dystopian novel. I'd forgotten how much fun they can be. Yes, Branded is YA and considering I'm bordering on 31, I do like more 'risque' books, however, Branded is not as spic and span as you may be lead to believe. The blood, sweat and tears within this book is not something for the faint at heart.<br><br>Really the only thing that makes this a YA is the fact that there isn't much swearing (or none - but I speak under correction). There are no sexual themed naked scenes so that would add to it being considered a YA... but other than that it's pretty dark, deep and emotional... Quite grown up. But you know what... even though I do love my angst and passion... I didn't miss it at all while reading this book. It was only afterwards that I realized there was no adult content and even then, I can't say it bothered me at all nor did it change my opinion of the book.<br><br>I don't need to go into what Branded is about because the summary is sufficient enough to give you a taste, however, I feel it is my duty to inform you that if you have not gotten your hands on this book yet... do so immediately. It's so engrossing and perfectly written that for those few hours while you are reading this book... you are gripped into the unique world created by Abi &amp; Missy within Branded.<br><br>I have absolutely no complaints. None what-so-ever... ok maybe one and that's is that I really need to get my hands on the second part. Although Branded doesn't end on a cliffer, you don't get nearly enough of Cole...<br><br>Who is this Cole I speak of? Well... Cole is the reading worlds newest book boyfriend. Perfect and Divine! <br><br>I loved every single character in the book... well except for the Commander and we aren't suppose to like him so clearly the job of character development was done brilliantly.<br><br>Branded is a debut novel for author duo Abi Ketner &amp; Missy Kalicicki and what a privilege to have been able to read it.<br><br>I will never be the same again... I too have been Branded... <br><br> <br><br>♥ <i>

Branded gave me so many feels.<br/><br/>The Hole is definitely one of the last places I'd ever want to be, and it was described in such detail that I was frightened for Lexi and even a tad shaken myself.   <b>5/5 Stars</b>
</p><br />Branded is fast paced, action packed with a slight amount of gore and heartbreak. Branded gave me so many feels.<br /><br />The Hole is definitely one of the last places I'd ever want to be, and it was described in such detail that I was frightened for Lexi and even a tad shaken myself. The world created by Abi and Missy was extremely terrifying.<br /><br />I loved Lexi, she puked A TON but ended up super strong and badass. Also, COLEXI! I love them together, and they aren't your conventional YA angsty couple, they stay together and fight for each other. Its really admirable, and I couldn't wait for the next book, Hunted, to see them kick tons more ass together. Theres tons of chemistry and passion between them.<br /><br />I was extremely happy with Branded and I think most YA dystopian fans will be too!</span>

    <a title="Zakirrah BookBlogger" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15894726-zakirrah-bookblogger"><img alt="Zakirrah BookBlogger" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396291066p2/15894726.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/614321805?book_show_action=true">May 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zakirrah BookBlogger" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zakirrah BookBlogger" href="/user/show/15894726-zakirrah-bookblogger">Zakirrah BookBlogger</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15894726-zakirrah-bookblogger?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer614321805" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7135291719696548597"><b>5 BRILLIANT, HEART RACING,CAPTIVATING DYSTOPIAN STARS<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421420ra/837112.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>"Never did I imagine they’d come for me. Never did I imagine all those nights I heard them dragging someone else away that I’d join them."</b><br/><br/>The book is set post World War V. The commander, a cold hearted man who wants to eradicate all sins by locking up sinners in a place called The Hole,there is no trial.He has took over the country and everyone is under his control.Anyone who speaks out against him will be branded a sinner or executed.<br/><br/><b>"You can</b></span>
  <span id="freeText7135291719696548597" style="display:none"><b>5 BRILLIANT, HEART RACING,CAPTIVATING DYSTOPIAN STARS<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421420ra/837112.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>"Never did I imagine they’d come for me. Never did I imagine all those nights I heard them dragging someone else away that I’d join them."</b><br><br>The book is set post World War V. The commander, a cold hearted man who wants to eradicate all sins by locking up sinners in a place called The Hole,there is no trial.He has took over the country and everyone is under his control.Anyone who speaks out against him will be branded a sinner or executed.<br><br><b>"You can overcome anything...short of death."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412067i/810161._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lexi Hamilton has been accused and guards have come to take her away to The Hole,she doesn't have a chance to defend herself..there is no trial.Screaming that she has been falsely accused would result in torture or death.She is branded around her neck with <i>LUST</i>.She may not have committed the crime but The Hole is now her new home.Survival is key.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421420i/837113._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>The Seven Deadly Sins:<br>Lust ~ Blue<br>Gluttony ~ Orange<br>Greed ~ Yellow<br>Sloth ~ Black<br>Wrath ~ Red<br>Envy ~ Green<br>Pride ~ Purple </b><br><br>This is an awesome,fast paced, heart wrenching romance.I was sucked into this imaginary world right from page 1.I was captivated by the environment, the disturbing scenes and the story. I'm sure The Hole is just another word for Hell! It is so creepy,gritty and made my skin crawl.<br><br><b>"I don't want to die, but at the same time, I wish I were dead."</b><br><br>Lexi Hamilton is a strong, brave fighter.She fights for survival and for freedom.You couldn't help but sympathise with her, can you imagine this even happening to you? :O <br><br><b>The Hole can’t keep me. The Hole can’t break me. <br>I am more than my brand. I’m a fighter. <br>My name is Lexi Hamilton, and this is my story.</b><br><br>She is assigned a guard to watch her. Cole is a strong, loyal(don't forget hot) guard ;) He isn't like most of the guards, who treat sinners like dirt. In the midst of chaos a relationship is formed between guard and sinner. Lexi and Cole's feelings become stronger as days go by but its wrong. For a Guard to love a Sinner is like committing suicide in the worst possible way.If they are accused they will be tortured and killed. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380410795ra/805990.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>"Shhh..." He grips me closer to his body and then softly whispers in my ear, "I'm about to kiss you, and once I start I won't be able to stop. Just thought I should warn you."</b><br><br>Now lets get down to the important character in this book...Zeus ;)<br>The loving protective awesome dog! I loved this dog he is always there for Lexi when she needs him!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421420ra/837114.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Abi Ketner and Missy Kalicicki did a superb job with this book I cant wait for more! I want to know more about Cole!<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380824035i/3125929._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380824035i/3125930._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>**ARC courtesy of the authors via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review**<br><br><b>Check out my blog for more reviews!<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://zakirrahsbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://zakirrahsbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br><br>Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Zakirrahs-Book-Blog/486887338054979">https://www.facebook.com/pages/Zakirr...</a></b></span>

<div id="review_964042979" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/964042979" />
    <a title="Rachel" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13329837-rachel"><img alt="Rachel" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1570954636p2/13329837.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/964042979?book_show_action=true">Jun 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel" href="/user/show/13329837-rachel">Rachel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22608435-branded">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13329837-rachel?shelf=ebooks-i-own">ebooks-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13329837-rachel?shelf=received-for-review">received-for-review</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer964042979" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3472936773190147691"><br/><br/>I don't like to hurt people's feelings, but when I'm asked to review a book, I give my honest opinion. I agreed to review this book even though I'm not a fan of dystopian lit.<br/><br/>First of all, the writing was poor AT BEST. This book could have used SO many more revisions. There were a LOT of pacing problems. It was lackluster and poorly worded, not to mention the grammar problems. <br/><br/>Second, to me, this book felt like a rip-off of every other dystopian book I've read. It seemed like a mash-up of Shatte</span>
  <span id="freeText3472936773190147691" style="display:none"><br /><br />I don't like to hurt people's feelings, but when I'm asked to review a book, I give my honest opinion. I agreed to review this book even though I'm not a fan of dystopian lit.<br /><br />First of all, the writing was poor AT BEST. This book could have used SO many more revisions. There were a LOT of pacing problems. It was lackluster and poorly worded, not to mention the grammar problems. <br /><br />Second, to me, this book felt like a rip-off of every other dystopian book I've read. It seemed like a mash-up of Shatter Me, Divergent and The Host...among others. There was nothing original here. Even the love story was cliche and tired.<br /><br />Lastly, I didn't feel anything for the characters. They weren't developed. I was bored with the story. I figured out the twist. I just wanted it to end. I wouldn't have finished it, had I not agreed to review it.<br /><br />I liked the dog.<br /><br />I was not impressed and will be more careful with the books I agree to review. Thank you for asking me to review this, but please don't ask for a review unless you want my honest opinion. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3472936773190147691" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_558859474" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/558859474" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/558859474?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=thriller">thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=actiony">actiony</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=dystopia">dystopia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-book-1">series-book-1</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer558859474" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1914772293730841545"><b>Wow! What an utterly thrilling, heartbreaking, brutally intense read! I loved it!</b><br/><br/>The story is set in a future dystopian world which is ruled by ‘The Commander’. The Commander believes that the seven deadly sins were the downfall of society, and therefore anybody even <u>accused</u> of committing one of these sins is immediately labelled a Sinner, branded around the neck with the colour representative of the sin they have been accused of committing, and thrown into ‘The Hole’ – a horrifyingly violent pr</span>
  <span id="freeText1914772293730841545" style="display:none"><b>Wow! What an utterly thrilling, heartbreaking, brutally intense read! I loved it!</b><br /><br />The story is set in a future dystopian world which is ruled by ‘The Commander’. The Commander believes that the seven deadly sins were the downfall of society, and therefore anybody even <u>accused</u> of committing one of these sins is immediately labelled a Sinner, branded around the neck with the colour representative of the sin they have been accused of committing, and thrown into ‘The Hole’ – a horrifyingly violent prison community where you are sentenced to live, work, and die.<br /><br />When 18 year old Lexi is accused of the sin of Lust, she is taken from her home, branded, and sent to The Hole. With her blue brand giving the impression that she is a whore, she becomes an instant target for the prisoners and guards behind the walls, but she has one thing in her favour. A permanent guard - Cole. <br /><br />Lexi is amazing!!! Despite her devastatingly traumatic past, and her horrific present, she doesn’t give up. She carries on with her life, trying to survive in the worst of circumstances, and her strength despite all that she endures makes you want to stand up and cheer for her.<br /><br /><i>“You can overcome anything...short of death.”</i><br /><br />And Cole… well, Cole is freaking phenomenal! Strong, brave, and determined to protect Lexi at all costs, he guards her well, treating her with respect and care, like she is somebody worthy, and that is something she has not had for a very long time – even before she came to The Hole. Plus he has the most awesome dog ever – Zeus is a total scene stealer. His protectiveness over Lexi is gorgeous!<br /><br />But the two of them face great danger when they start to develop feelings for each other. Relationships between guards and sinners is strictly forbidden, and that lesson is demonstrated in shocking brutality early on in the book. So even though Cole acts like her guard in public, things are very different when they are alone. And they are justifiably terrified. <br /><br /><i>“I want you to trust me. I need you to trust me.” He sighs and I hear the pain and confusion in his voice.<br />“Why?”<br />“I don’t know why and it scares the hell out of me.”</i><br /> <br />But suffering through violence, death, heartbreak and brutal attacks only draws them closer together <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ the scene in the shower when he is washing her after she is attacked almost had me in tears! So innocent, but SO MUCH EMOTION!!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, and despite the danger, the most beautiful, sweet and tender (YA) romance begins to develop.<br /><br /><i>“Shhh…” He grips me closer to his body and then softly whispers in my ear, “I’m about to kiss you, and once I start I won’t be able to stop. Just thought I should warn you.”</i><br /><br />I love that Lexi and Cole were able to fall for each other despite the brutality of everything happening around them. The connection between them is gorgeous, and while the romance is an important part of the story, it doesn’t overwhelm everything else that is going on. And there is SO much going on – not only the daily battle to survive, but also the ongoing threat of danger, an evil dictator, and a looming rebellion. <br /><br />But even with all of this unfolding, there was definitely enough swoon to satisfy the romance-lover in me. <br /><br /><i>“I don’t ever want you to question it. I love you. I’d give my life to save yours. That’s how much I love you. Don’t you dare ever doubt that.”<br /><br />“Even if it was only for a day, an hour, or a minute – I would risk everything just so I could be with you.”<br /><br />“ <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I’m here with you and all of a sudden my life makes sense again. The way you look at me makes me feel human – not a lifeless soul trapped in my own skin. So I thank you from the bottom of my heart for saving me, reviving me, caring for me, but most of all, for being my friend. I’m a train wreck – I know this – but with you by my side, I’m starting to mend.<br />So please, don’t give up on me. I need you to remind me every day who I really am and what I can become. If you can find it in your heart to love me, then please don’t run away. Promise me you’ll stay. Even though we can’t ever be together, promise me you’ll stay.<br />I never knew what it felt like to be in love, and I never wanted to until I fell in love with you.<br />I love you. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></i>” <br /><br />SWOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOON!<br /><br />There is a sensational cast of characters. Both good and bad, they are well developed, and brilliantly written, and each play an important part of the story. Shout out to Sutton and Bruno. If I was living in that environment, I’d definitely want them on my side. And as for the bad guys – oh so EVIL!!! And totally stab-worthy. <br /><br />The story is fast-paced, full of action and absolutely thrilling. The writing is fantastic, the world is explained well and it’s beautifully descriptive - I could see the whole story unfolding in front of me like I was watching a movie, and I felt like I was experiencing it all alongside the characters. There are some sensational twists, and some big shocks that I totally didn’t see coming! And I love that the element of surprise was there! The authors definitely don’t hold back when it comes to describing the violence and hopelessness of the world, and shocking the reader, but in between all of the brutality, there are some beautifully tender moments which had me clutching my heart.<br /><br />Now for the ranty part - there is a part of the story towards the end of the book that I thought was completely stupid and unnecessary. I didn’t understand why it was written like that, and to be honest, it really pissed me off! (Be warned, this is a very spoilery rant – don’t read it unless you’ve already read the book. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Lexi and Cole’s separation at the end! WTF? I don’t get it! I just don’t get it! Why couldn’t they be together? Why did Lexi have to choose? I understand her wanting to fight for her freedom, and her right to be with Cole, but why did she have to be apart from him to do it? He was fighting for the same thing! I get that we, as readers, had to see her loyalty to Keegan, and I appreciate that, but she could have done that with Cole still by her side. To me, it didn't feel 'right' considering all that had come before it, and felt like it was thrown in there just to add unnecessary angst! And it bought the awesomeness of the book down for me. Ugh! OK, rant over.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>).<br /><br />All ends well though! There is a (mostly) happy ending, and while the book has a natural conclusion, there is definitely more of the story to come!<br /><br />I'm looking forward to more from this series.<br /><br />4 stars.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1914772293730841545" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3898049-heather?shelf=sex-pg-13">sex-pg-13</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer654116772" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3236433471581362417"><img alt='' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425914i/850411.jpg' width='284' height='413' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><p>What would you do if you lived in a world where you were guilty if you were accused? If you were branded for life for sins you did not commit? If you were thrown into a horrible prison called The Hole to fend for yourself and fight daily to survive? This is the horror and the hell that Abi Ketner and Missy Kalicicki created in Branded.</p><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><p>Lexi is a young woman who has been forced into the Hole and branded for committing the sin of Lust. She is immediately given a guard and escorted to h</p></span>
  <span id="freeText3236433471581362417" style="display:none"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425914i/850411.jpg" width="284" height="413" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><p>What would you do if you lived in a world where you were guilty if you were accused? If you were branded for life for sins you did not commit? If you were thrown into a horrible prison called The Hole to fend for yourself and fight daily to survive? This is the horror and the hell that Abi Ketner and Missy Kalicicki created in Branded.</p><br><span>[image error]</span><br><p>Lexi is a young woman who has been forced into the Hole and branded for committing the sin of Lust. She is immediately given a guard and escorted to her new "home". She learns the rules in The Hole. She is is fortunate enough to have been given an assignment in the hospital.</p><br><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427225i/854042._SY540_.jpg" width="222" height="298" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><p>Cole is her guard and she soon discovers that this is not the norm in The Hole. She is very grateful for his protection. Sinners branded with Lust are frequently given the "job" of being a prostitute. She escaped that fate and is sent to work daily. She is leered at and she discovers that without protection, she would become a frequent victim to the depravity that surrounds her.</p><br><p>Cole saves her time and again. He is a handsome guard who soon discovers that Lexi is not all that she seems. Lexi soon discovers that The Hole is not all that it seems and Cole becomes someone who she finds herself falling for.</p><br><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427225i/854043._SY540_.jpg" width="174" height="263" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><p>In The Hole the biggest sin is falling for a sinner. Both the sinner and the guard are dealt with swiftly and painfully. The guards take their frustrations out on the sinners. They are viewed as sub-humans. The Commander is the ultimate authority and he is the man behind the current system. He is never seen but he is all seeing. The atmosphere is one of fear and hate.</p><br><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427225i/854044.jpg" width="357" height="236" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><p>For some people in The Hole, all hope is lost and they simply give up. But for a few, they dream of a better future. Of crystal clear blue waters and sunny skies. They know that they can be more and have more for themselves and the future generations. They are the roots that take hold and refuse to be pulled.</p><br><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427225i/854045._SX540_.jpg" width="310" height="207" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><p>This book was <strong>EPIC</strong>! This is the <strong>DEBUT</strong> novel for both authors. It was simply amazing. This was slightly off genre for me. This is a young adult dystopian fantasy. It is all story with a love story in the mix. There were no graphic scenes and I would rate it PG-13. I usually go for the more adult stuff but I did not find this one missing anything at all.</p><br><p>
  <strong>It was simply magnificent.</strong>
</p><br><img alt="" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380427225ra/854046.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><p>Great job! 5 Stars!</p><br><p>
  <a href="http://johnstohbibliomaniac.files.wordpress.com/2013/05/red_star_5_of_5-bb0a37528bbb2ff1f4b732afff2bb9681.png" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img alt="red_star_5_of_5-bb0a37528bbb2ff1f4b732afff2bb968" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380378039i/733461.png" width="75" height="15" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</p><br><p>***A copy of this book was provided by the publisher via NetGalley in exchange for a fair and honest review.***</p><br><br></span>

<div id="review_544159769" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/544159769" />
    <a title="Kendall {Book Crazy}" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11385469-kendall-book-crazy"><img alt="Kendall {Book Crazy}" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514724413p2/11385469.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/544159769?book_show_action=true">Feb 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kendall {Book Crazy}" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kendall {Book Crazy}" href="/user/show/11385469-kendall-book-crazy">Kendall {Book Crazy}</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11385469-kendall-book-crazy?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11385469-kendall-book-crazy?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer544159769" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2765177843503899322"><i>"You're amazing just the way you are. There's not a single thing I would change about you. When you smile my entire world stops. All I see is you. I need you."</i><br/><br/>For a debut novel, this one really blew me away! I sometimes cringe when I read a debut novel as sometimes authors have to find comfort in writing, but with Branded I could tell that the authors felt passionate and comfortable while writing it! I had been wanting to read Branded since I first heard about it after one of the authors approac</span>
  <span id="freeText2765177843503899322" style="display:none"><i>"You're amazing just the way you are. There's not a single thing I would change about you. When you smile my entire world stops. All I see is you. I need you."</i><br /><br />For a debut novel, this one really blew me away! I sometimes cringe when I read a debut novel as sometimes authors have to find comfort in writing, but with Branded I could tell that the authors felt passionate and comfortable while writing it! I had been wanting to read Branded since I first heard about it after one of the authors approached me about reading the first chapter! I normally don't like just reading the first few chapters of a book because then I'm even more desperate to read the whole thing! With Branded I wasn't sure what to expect as it didn't have a cover or a synopsis at that point, but I soon became addicted! Once I started reading this book, I couldn't stop so when I got an ARC of it I screamed! This book is not for the fainthearted! It's bloody and gory and full of suspense! It's definitely for someone who loves an adventure or for someone who loves discovering something new! The plot of Branded really blew me away! It was a fresh idea with new elements added and there was so much going on in it! I did cry several times during it as well! I knew that I was going to, but I tried so hard not too! It really hits you hard and it really will make your heart break! The suspense throughout this book really was mind-blowing as well! It felt like I was watching my favourite action film for the first time! You know, when your eyes are glued to the screen and you can't look away! Well, with Branded I was hooked from page one and I couldn't stop reading until I got to the last page! What I enjoyed about this book was that I found out things that I thought that I wasn't going too! I thought that some of it would have carried over to the next book, but that actually probably won't happen as secrets get revealed in this book and then resolved! The characters were also amazing! I couldn't help but feel sorry for Lexi as she had been through so much and then when she gets put in The Hole my heart broke for her! As I discovered her story I started to feel so much more for her! I connected with her the whole way through this book and that connection didn't break once! Cole was so hot! I loved that he was in nearly all the scenes and he had such a big role as he was my favourite male character! Cole would do anything for Lexi and you could see that everytime he was with her! It was so sweet, but in Lexi's world you really needed something beautiful and for me that was it! I am definitely going to read the next book in this series and I will probably be begging the authors to let me read any chapter from it! I saw the original cover for this book and I have to be honest and say that I adored that cover, but after reading Branded I can see how well the new cover suits it! Huge thank you to Abi and Missy for an ARC of Branded! </span>
  <a data-text-id="2765177843503899322" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
